\"GetBasicRoles\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Grafana codebase implements the three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) across several interconnected layers:\\n\\n## 1. Role Type Definition\\n\\n**`pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`** is the canonical definition of the three-tier model. It defines `RoleType` as a string type with constants `RoleViewer`, `RoleEditor`, `RoleAdmin` (and `RoleNone`). The `rolePrecedence` map assigns numeric weights (Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40), and the `Includes` method implements hierarchical role checking (Admin includes Editor includes Viewer). The `Parents()` and `Children()` methods enumerate the role hierarchy.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/org/model.go`** re-exports these constants as `org.RoleViewer`, `org.RoleEditor`, `org.RoleAdmin` for use throughout the codebase, and defines `OrgUser` which stores a user's role in an organization.\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`** contains `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()` which creates the in-memory map of basic role definitions (admin, editor, viewer, none, grafana_admin) as `RoleDTO` objects. `DeclareFixedRoles()` registers fixed RBAC roles with their grants to org roles. `BuiltInRolesWithParents()` expands a set of roles to include all parent roles (e.g., granting to Editor also grants to Admin).\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go`** is the core RBAC service. `registerRolesLocked()` processes role registrations and appends permissions to the appropriate basic role's permission list using `BuiltInRolesWithParents`. `getUserPermissions()` assembles a user's effective permissions by combining their basic role's permissions (from the in-memory map) with database-stored managed/fixed role permissions. `DeclareFixedRoles()` validates and stores role registrations.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/database/database.go`** contains the SQL query `basicRoleAssignsSQL` that joins `builtin_role` with `org_user` on the role column to resolve which RBAC roles apply to a user based on their org role (Viewer/Editor/Admin).\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`** provides the primary RBAC middleware. `Middleware()` wraps an `Evaluator` into an HTTP handler that calls `authorize()`. `authorize()` injects URL parameters into scope templates and calls `ac.Evaluate()`. `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware()` handles cross-org authorization. The `deny()` function returns 403 responses.\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/auth.go`** provides the legacy role-based guard. `RoleAuth()` checks if the user's `OrgRole` matches any of the specified roles. `Auth()` handles signed-in and Grafana admin checks.\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/middleware.go`** declares the pre-built middleware guards: `ReqEditorRole = RoleAuth(org.RoleEditor, org.RoleAdmin)` and `ReqOrgAdmin = RoleAuth(org.RoleAdmin)`, which are used throughout the API routing.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/apiserver/auth/authorizer/role.go`** implements a Kubernetes-style authorizer (`roleAuthorizer.Authorize()`) that maps org roles to k8s verbs: Admin allows all verbs, Editor allows read/write/create/delete/update, Viewer allows only get/list/watch.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/accesscontrol.go`** implements `AccessControl.Evaluate()` which checks a user's permission map against an evaluator, with scope resolution via registered resolvers.\\n\\n## 4. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`** defines the three action tiers for dashboards: `DashboardViewActions` (read), `DashboardEditActions` (read+write+delete), `DashboardAdminActions` (read+write+delete+permissions). `registerDashboardRoles()` declares fixed roles `fixed:dashboards:viewer/editor/admin` granted to the corresponding org roles. `ProvideDashboardPermissions()` configures the `InheritedScopesSolver` to walk up the folder tree for permission inheritance.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`** similarly defines `FolderViewActions`, `FolderEditActions`, `FolderAdminActions` and registers `fixed:folders:viewer/editor/admin` roles. The `InheritedScopesSolver` calls `dashboards.GetInheritedScopes()` to resolve parent folder scopes.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`** implements the scope resolution chain. `GetInheritedScopes()` walks up the folder hierarchy via `folderSvc.GetParents()` and returns all ancestor folder scopes. `NewFolderUIDScopeResolver()` and `NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver()` register scope attribute resolvers that expand a single folder/dashboard scope into the full inheritance chain. `resolveDashboardScope()` combines dashboard scope with its folder and all ancestor folder scopes.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/dashboards/service/dashboard_service.go`** implements `SetDefaultPermissions()` and `SetDefaultPermissionsAfterCreate()` which assign default permissions when a dashboard/folder is created: the creating user gets Admin, `org.RoleEditor` gets Edit, `org.RoleViewer` gets View (for root-level resources).\\n\\n**`pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go`** implements `NewAccessControlDashboardPermissionFilter()` which generates SQL WHERE clauses for dashboard/folder queries based on a user's RBAC permissions, supporting both direct permissions and inherited folder permissions via recursive CTEs.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/accesscontrol/dashboard_permissions.go`** defines `dashboardPermissionTranslation` and `folderPermissionTranslation` maps that translate legacy `PERMISSION_VIEW/EDIT/ADMIN` values into RBAC action sets, and the `dashboardPermissionsMigrator` that migrates legacy ACL entries to RBAC permissions.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go`** and **`store.go`** provide the generic resource permissions service used by both dashboard and folder permission services. `SetBuiltInRolePermission()` sets permissions for a built-in role (Viewer/Editor/Admin) on a specific resource. `GetPermissions()` retrieves permissions including inherited scopes.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/authz/rbac/mapper.go`** maps Kubernetes API verbs to RBAC actions for dashboards and folders, including action set mappings (e.g., `dashboards:view`, `folders:edit`, `folders:admin`) that correspond to the three permission tiers.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/authz/zanzana/translations.go`** maps the three org roles to OpenFGA relation types (`basic_viewer`, `basic_editor`, `basic_admin`) for the Zanzibar-based authorization backend.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/rbac_sync.go`** syncs RBAC permissions into the user's identity during authentication via `SyncPermissionsHook()`.\\n\\n**`pkg/services/authz/rbac/store/store.go`** provides `GetBasicRoles()` which retrieves a user's basic role (Viewer/Editor/Admin) from the database for the RBAC authorization service.\\n\\n**`pkg/setting/setting.go`** configures `AutoAssignOrgRole` which defaults new users to Viewer, Editor, or Admin, enforcing the three-tier model at user creation time.\\n\\n**`pkg/login/social/connectors/org_role_mapper.go`** maps external OAuth/SAML group memberships to Grafana org roles (Viewer/Editor/Admin) via `OrgRoleMapper.MapOrgRoles()`.\\n\\nAdditional files that declare fixed roles for specific subsystems using the three-tier grants pattern include: `pkg/api/accesscontrol.go` (HTTP API roles), `pkg/services/ngalert/accesscontrol.go` (alerting roles), `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/manager/roles.go` (service account roles), and `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginaccesscontrol/accesscontrol.go` (plugin roles).\"\n}\n",
